59   def getNodeTypes(nodes: Map[String, TRAPIQueryNode]): Map[String, IRI] =
60     nodes
61       .map(entry =>
62         (entry._2.category, entry._2.id) match {
63           case (_, Some(c))    => List(entry._1 -> c)
64           case (Some(t), None) => List(entry._1 -> t.iri)
65           case (None, None)    => Nil
66         })
67       .flatten
68       .toMap
69 
70   def run(limit: Option[Int],
71           submittedQueryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], List[QuerySolution]] = {
72     val queryGraph = enforceQueryEdgeTypes(submittedQueryGraph)
73     val nodeTypes = getNodeTypes(queryGraph.nodes)
74     for {
75       predicates <- ZIO.foreachPar(queryGraph.edges.filter(edge => edge._2.predicate.nonEmpty)) { (k, v) =>
76         for {
77           foundPredicates <- getTRAPIQEdgePredicates(v)
78           predicates = foundPredicates.map(a => sparql" $a ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
79           edgeIDVar = Var(k)
80           edgeSourceVar = Var(v.subject)
81           edgeTargetVar = Var(v.`object`)
82           sparqlChunk =
83             sparql"""
84                  VALUES $edgeIDVar { $predicates }
85                  $edgeSourceVar $edgeIDVar $edgeTargetVar .
86               """
87         } yield (v, sparqlChunk)
88       }
89       (edges, sparqlLines) = predicates.unzip
90       nodesToDirectTypes =
91         queryGraph.nodes
92           .map { node =>
93             val nodeVar = Var(node._1)
94             val nodeTypeVar = Var(s"${node._1}_type")
95             sparql""" $nodeVar $SesameDirectType $nodeTypeVar .  """
96           }
97           .fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
98       projectionVariableNames = queryGraph.edges.flatMap(entry => List(entry._1)) ++ edges.flatMap(e =>
99         List(e.subject, e.`object`)) ++ queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => s"${entry._1}_type")
100       projection = projectionVariableNames.map(Var(_)).map(v => sparql" $v ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
101       moreLines = for {
102         id <- edges.flatMap(a => List(a.subject, a.`object`))
103         subjVar = Var(id)
104         v <- nodeTypes.get(id)
105       } yield sparql"$subjVar $RDFType $v ."
106       valuesClause = (sparqlLines ++ moreLines).fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
107       limitValue = limit.getOrElse(1000)
108       limitSparql = if (limitValue > 0) sparql" LIMIT $limitValue" else sparql""
109       queryString = sparql"""
110                           SELECT DISTINCT $projection
111                           WHERE {
112                             $nodesToDirectTypes
113                             $valuesClause
114                           }
115                           $limitSparql
116                           """
117       response <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryString.toQuery)
118     } yield response
119   }
120 
121   def enforceQueryEdgeTypes(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph): TRAPIQueryGraph = {
122     val improvedEdgeMap = queryGraph.edges.map { case (edgeID, edge) =>
123       val newPredicate = edge.predicate match {
124         case None          => Some(BiolinkPredicate("related_to"))
125         case somePredicate => somePredicate
126       }
127       edgeID -> edge.copy(predicate = newPredicate)
128     }
129     queryGraph.copy(edges = improvedEdgeMap)
130   }
131 
132   def getTRAPIEdgeKey(pred: Option[BiolinkPredicate], sub: String, obj: String) = {
133     val edgeKey = TRAPIEdgeKey(pred, sub, obj).asJson.deepDropNullValues.noSpaces
134     String.format("%064x", new BigInteger(1, messageDigest.digest(edgeKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))))
135   }

137   def parseResultSet(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
138                      querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], TRAPIMessage] =
139     for {
140       biolinkData <- biolinkData
141       initialKGNodes <- getTRAPINodes(queryGraph, querySolutions)
142       initialKGEdges <- getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph, querySolutions)
143       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph, querySolutions)
144       trapiBindings <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
145         getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph, querySolution) zip Task.effect(querySolutionsToEdgeBindings(querySolution))
146       }
147       allEdgeBindings = trapiBindings.flatMap(_._2).toMap
148       allCamIds = allEdgeBindings.values.flatten.filter(a => a.provenance.isDefined).map(a => a.provenance.get)
149       prov2CAMStuffTripleMap <- ZIO.foreachPar(allCamIds)(prov => getCAMStuff(IRI(prov)).map(prov -> _)).map(_.toMap)
150       allCAMTriples = prov2CAMStuffTripleMap.values.to(Set).flatten
151       allTripleNodes = allCAMTriples.flatMap(t => Set(t.subj, t.obj))
152       slotStuffNodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allTripleNodes.to(List), biolinkData.classes)
153       extraKGNodes = getExtraKGNodes(allTripleNodes, slotStuffNodeDetails, biolinkData)
154       allPredicates = allCAMTriples.map(_.pred)
155       slotStuffList <- getSlotStuff(allPredicates.to(List))
156       extraKGEdges = allCAMTriples.flatMap { triple =>
157         for {
158           slotStuff <- slotStuffList.find(_.kid == triple.pred)
159           predBLTermOpt = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == slotStuff.biolinkSlot)
160         } yield getTRAPIEdgeKey(predBLTermOpt, triple.subj.value, triple.obj.value) -> TRAPIEdge(triple.subj, triple.obj, None, predBLTermOpt, None)
161       }.toMap
162 
163       results = trapiBindings.map { case (resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) => TRAPIResult(resultNodeBindings, resultEdgeBindings) }
164

168 //          provAndTRAPIResults <- ZIO.foreach(provsAndCamTriples) { (prov, triples) =>
169 //            for {
170 //              trapiResults <- ZIO.foreach(triples.zipWithIndex) { tripleAndIndex =>

172 //                  slotStuff <- ZIO.fromOption(slotStuffList.find(_.kid == tripleAndIndex._1.pred)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get slotstuff"))
173 //                  predBLTermOpt = biolinkData.predicates.find(a => a.iri == slotStuff.biolinkSlot)
174 //                  edgeKey = TRAPIEdgeKey(predBLTermOpt, tripleAndIndex._1.subj.value, tripleAndIndex._1.obj.value).asJson.deepDropNullValues.noSpaces
175 //                  encodedEdgeKey = String.format("%064x", new BigInteger(1, messageDigest.digest(edgeKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))))

188       finalResults = results //++ bindingResults.flatten
189 
190       trapiKGNodes = initialKGNodes ++ extraKGNodes
191       trapiKGEdges = initialKGEdges ++ extraKGEdges

193     } yield TRAPIMessage(Some(queryGraph), Some(TRAPIKnowledgeGraph(trapiKGNodes, trapiKGEdges)), Some(finalResults.distinct))

195    def getTRAPIEdges(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
196                             querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Map[String, TRAPIEdge]] =
197     for {
198       trapiEdges <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
199         for {
200           nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => (entry._1, IRI(querySolution.getResource(s"${entry._1}_type").getURI))))
201           edges <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (k, v) =>
202             for {
203               source <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(v.subject)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get source id"))
204               target <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(v.`object`)).orElseFail(new Exception("could not get target id"))
205             } yield getTRAPIEdgeKey(v.predicate, v.subject, v.`object`) -> TRAPIEdge(source, target, None, v.predicate, None)
206           }
207         } yield edges.toList
208       }
209     } yield trapiEdges.flatten.toMap
210 
211   def getTRAPINodes(
212     queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph,
213     querySolutions: List[QuerySolution]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Map[IRI, TRAPINode]] = {
214     val allOntClassIRIsZ = ZIO
215       .foreach(querySolutions) { qs =>
216         ZIO.foreach(qs.varNames.asScala.filter(_.endsWith("_type")).to(Iterable)) { typeVar =>
217           ZIO.effect(IRI(qs.getResource(typeVar).getURI)).mapError { e =>
218             new Exception(s"Value of _type variable $typeVar is not a URI", e)
219           }
220         }
221       }
222       .map(_.flatten)
223     for {
224       allOntClassIRIs <- allOntClassIRIsZ
225       biolinkData <- biolinkData
226       nodeDetails <- getTRAPINodeDetails(allOntClassIRIs, biolinkData.classes)
227       termToLabelAndTypes = nodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
228         val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
229         term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
230       }
231       trapiNodes <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
232         for {
233           nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(entry => (entry._1, querySolution.get(s"${entry._1}_type").toString)))
234           nodes <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.nodes) { (k, v) =>
235             for {
236               nodeIRI <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(k)).orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $k"))
237               labelAndTypes = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(IRI(nodeIRI), (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
238               (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = labelAndTypes
239               biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
240               nodeBiolinkTypes = biolinkData.classes.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
241             } yield IRI(nodeIRI) -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(nodeBiolinkTypes), None)
242           }
243         } yield nodes.toList
244       }
245     } yield trapiNodes.flatten.toMap
246   }
247 
248   private def getTRAPINodeDetails(
249     nodeIdList: List[IRI],
250     biolinkClasses: List[BiolinkClass]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType]] = {
251     val nodeIds = nodeIdList.map(n => sparql" $n ").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
252     for {
253       namedThingBiolinkClass <- ZIO
254         .fromOption(biolinkClasses.find(a => a.shorthand == "named_thing"))
255         .orElseFail(new Exception("Could not find BiolinkClass:NamedThing"))
256       // requiring biolinkType makes some terms not be found when these results are used elsewhere - must be handled there
257       queryText = sparql"""
258                        SELECT ?term ?biolinkType (MIN(?term_label) AS ?label)
259                        WHERE {
260                          VALUES ?term { $nodeIds }
261                          ?term $RDFSSubClassOf ?biolinkType .
262                          ?biolinkType $BiolinkMLIsA* ${namedThingBiolinkClass.iri} .
263                          OPTIONAL { ?term $RDFSLabel ?term_label }
264                        }
265                        GROUP BY ?term ?biolinkType
266                        """
267       termsAndBiolinkTypes <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType](queryText.toQuery)
268     } yield termsAndBiolinkTypes
269   }
270 
271   def getTRAPINodeBindings(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph, querySolution: QuerySolution): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig], Map[String, List[TRAPINodeBinding]]] =
272     for {
273       nodeMap <- Task.effect(queryGraph.nodes.map(n => (n._1, querySolution.get(s"${n._1}_type").toString)))
274       nodeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.nodes) { (k, v) =>
275         for {
276           nodeIRI <- ZIO.fromOption(nodeMap.get(k)).orElseFail(new Exception(s"Missing node IRI: $k"))
277         } yield k -> List(TRAPINodeBinding(IRI(nodeIRI)))
278       }
279     } yield nodeBindings

281   def getTRAPIEdgeBindingsMany(queryGraph: TRAPIQueryGraph, querySolutions: List[QuerySolution])
282     : ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient with Has[BiolinkData], Throwable, Map[QuerySolution, Map[String, List[TRAPIEdgeBinding]]]] = {
283     val solutionTriples = for {
284       queryEdge <- queryGraph.edges
285       solution <- querySolutions
286     } yield Triple(
287       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._2.subject).getURI),
288       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._1).getURI),
289       IRI(solution.getResource(queryEdge._2.`object`).getURI)
290     )
291     for {
292       provs <- getProvenance(solutionTriples.to(Set))
293       querySolutionsToEdgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(querySolutions) { querySolution =>
294         for {
295           edgeBindings <- ZIO.foreach(queryGraph.edges) { (k, v) =>
296             for {
297               predicateRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(k).toString)
298               sourceRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(v.subject).toString)
299               targetRDFNode <- Task.effect(querySolution.get(v.`object`).toString)
300               edgeKey = TRAPIEdgeKey(v.predicate, sourceRDFNode, targetRDFNode).asJson.deepDropNullValues.noSpaces
301               encodedTRAPIEdgeKey = String.format("%064x",
302                                                   new BigInteger(1, messageDigest.digest(edgeKey.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8))))
303               prov <-
304                 ZIO
305                   .fromOption(provs.get(TripleString(sourceRDFNode, predicateRDFNode, targetRDFNode)))
306                   .orElseFail(new Exception("Unexpected triple string"))
307             } yield k -> List(TRAPIEdgeBinding(encodedTRAPIEdgeKey, Some(prov)))
308           }
309         } yield querySolution -> edgeBindings
310       }
311     } yield querySolutionsToEdgeBindings.toMap
312   }
313 
314   private def getProvenance(edges: Set[Triple]): ZIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, Throwable, Map[TripleString, String]] = {
315     val values = edges.map(e => sparql"( ${e.subj} ${e.pred} ${e.obj} )").fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
316     val queryText =
317       sparql"""
318                 SELECT ?s ?p ?o ?g ?other
319                 WHERE {
320                   VALUES (?s ?p ?o) { $values }
321                   GRAPH ?g { ?s ?p ?o }
322                   OPTIONAL { ?g $ProvWasDerivedFrom ?other . }
323                 }
324               """
325     for {
326       bindings <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQuery(queryText.toQuery)
327       triplesToGraphs <- ZIO.foreach(bindings) { solution =>
328         Task.effect {
329           val graph = if (solution.contains("other")) solution.getResource("other").getURI else solution.getResource("g").getURI
330           val triple = TripleString(solution.getResource("s").getURI, solution.getResource("p").getURI, solution.getResource("o").getURI)
331           triple -> graph
332         }
333       }
334     } yield triplesToGraphs.toMap
335   }
336 
337   private def getCAMStuff(prov: IRI): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[Triple]] =
338     for {
339       queryText <- Task.effect(
340         sparql"""SELECT DISTINCT (?s_type AS ?subj) (?p AS ?pred) (?o_type AS ?obj) WHERE { GRAPH $prov {
341                      ?s ?p ?o .
342                      ?s $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
343                      ?o $RDFType $OWLNamedIndividual .
344                    }
345                    ?o $SesameDirectType ?o_type .
346                    ?s $SesameDirectType ?s_type .
347                    FILTER(isIRI(?o_type))
348                    FILTER(isIRI(?s_type))
349                  }"""
350       )
351       triples <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[Triple](queryText.toQuery)
352     } yield triples
353 
354   def getExtraKGNodes(camNodes: Set[IRI],
355                               slotStuffNodeDetails: List[TermWithLabelAndBiolinkType],
356                               biolinkData: BiolinkData): Map[IRI, TRAPINode] = {
357     val termToLabelAndTypes = slotStuffNodeDetails.groupBy(_.term).map { case (term, termsAndTypes) =>
358       val (labels, biolinkTypes) = termsAndTypes.map(t => t.label -> t.biolinkType).unzip
359       term -> (labels.flatten.headOption, biolinkTypes)
360     }
361     val nodeMap = camNodes.map { node =>
362       val (labelOpt, biolinkTypes) = termToLabelAndTypes.getOrElse(node, (None, List(BiolinkNamedThing)))
363       val biolinkTypesSet = biolinkTypes.to(Set)
364       val classes = biolinkData.classes.filter(c => biolinkTypesSet(c.iri))
365       node -> TRAPINode(labelOpt, Some(classes), None)
366     }.toMap
367     nodeMap
368   }
369 
370   private def getSlotStuff(predicates: List[IRI]): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[SlotStuff]] = {
371     val values = predicates.zipWithIndex
372       .map { case (p, i) =>
373         val id = StringUtils.leftPad(i.toString, 4, '0')
374         val qid = s"e$id"
375         sparql" ( $p $qid ) "
376       }
377       .fold(sparql"")(_ + _)
378     val queryText = sparql"""
379                      SELECT DISTINCT ?qid ?kid ?biolinkSlot ?label
380                      WHERE {
381                      VALUES (?kid ?qid) { $values }
382                      ?kid $SlotMapping ?biolinkSlot .
383                      ?biolinkSlot a $BiolinkMLSlotDefinition .
384                      OPTIONAL { ?kid $RDFSLabel ?label . }
385                      FILTER NOT EXISTS {
386                        ?kid $SlotMapping ?other .
387                        ?other $BiolinkMLIsA+/<https://w3id.org/biolink/biolinkml/meta/mixins>* ?biolinkSlot .
388                        }
389                      }
390                      """
391     SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[SlotStuff](queryText.toQuery)
392   }
393 
394   private def getTRAPIQEdgePredicates(edge: TRAPIQueryEdge): RIO[ZConfig[AppConfig] with HttpClient, List[IRI]] =
395     for {
396       edgeType <- ZIO.fromOption(edge.predicate).orElseFail(new Exception("failed to get edge type"))
397       queryText = sparql"""
398                    SELECT DISTINCT ?predicate
399                    WHERE {
400                      ?predicate $SlotMapping ${edgeType.iri} .
401                    }
402                    """
403       predicates <- SPARQLQueryExecutor.runSelectQueryAs[Predicate](queryText.toQuery)
404     } yield predicates.map(_.predicate)
